 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>S<SMALL>ECTION</SMALL> 16(<SMALL>A</SMALL>) B<SMALL>ENEFICIAL</SMALL> O<SMALL>WNERSHIP</SMALL>
R<SMALL>EPORTING</SMALL> C<SMALL>OMPLIANCE</SMALL> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Section 16(a) of the Exchange Act requires the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers,
and persons who own more than ten percent of a registered class of the Company&#146;s equity securities, to file with the SEC initial reports of ownership and reports of changes in ownership of common stock and other equity securities of the
Company. Officers, directors and greater than ten percent stockholders are required by SEC regulation to furnish the Company with copies of all Section 16(a) forms they file. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To the Company&#146;s knowledge, based solely on a review of the copies of such reports furnished to the Company and written representations that no other
reports were required, during the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016, all Section 16(a) filing requirements applicable to its officers, directors and greater than ten percent beneficial owners were satisfied. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">26 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Employment, Severance and Change in Control Agreements </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Employment and Agreements with Current Named Executive Officers </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have employment agreements with each of our current named executive officers. The agreements generally provide for
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">at-will</FONT> employment and set forth the executive officer&#146;s initial base salary, annual performance bonus opportunity, initial equity grant amount and eligibility for employee benefits. The key terms of the
offer letters are described below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Private Eiger entered into an employment agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Cory in December 2008. The agreement is for an
unspecified term and entitles Mr.&nbsp;Cory to an initial annual base salary of $320,000. Mr.&nbsp;Cory&#146;s current annual base salary is $431,250. The agreement also provides that he will be eligible to receive a bonus of up to 30% of base
salary based upon his performance and the attainment of company objectives. Pursuant to the terms of the agreement, Mr.&nbsp;Cory is subject to certain confidentiality obligations and is obligated to sign and comply with an agreement relating to
proprietary information and inventions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Private Eiger entered into an offer letter agreement with Dr.&nbsp;Quan in April 2015. The agreement is for an
unspecified term and entitles Dr.&nbsp;Quan to an initial annual base salary of $335,000. Dr.&nbsp;Quan&#146;s current annual base salary is $338,750. The agreement also provides that Dr.&nbsp;Quan will be eligible to receive a bonus of up to 30% of
base salary based upon her performance and the attainment of company objectives. Pursuant to the terms of the agreement, Dr.&nbsp;Quan is subject to certain confidentiality obligations and is obligated to sign and comply with an agreement relating
to proprietary information and inventions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Private Eiger entered into an offer letter agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer in September 2015. The agreement is
for an unspecified term and entitles Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer to an initial annual base salary of $300,000. Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer&#146;s current annual base salary is $330,000. The agreement also provides that Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer will be eligible to receive a bonus
of up to 35% of base salary based upon his performance and the attainment of company objectives. Pursuant to the terms of the agreement, Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer is subject to certain confidentiality obligations and is obligated to sign and comply with an
agreement relating to proprietary information and inventions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Potential Payments upon Termination of Employment or Change in Control with our Current
Named Executive Officers </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the terms of his employment agreement, upon termination of his employment without cause or upon a change in
control of Eiger that requires a move of the company over 60 miles or results in a substantial reduction in his responsibilities or compensation, Mr.&nbsp;Cory receives 12 months of base salary and COBRA coverage, as well as accelerated vesting of
his equity awards. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the terms of her offer letter agreement, upon a change in control of Eiger that requires a move of the company over 50
miles or results in a substantial reduction in her responsibilities or compensation, Dr.&nbsp;Quan receives 12 months of base salary, six months of COBRA coverage and the unvested portion of her equity awards will immediately vest in full. Upon
termination of her employment without cause, Dr.&nbsp;Quan receives six months of base salary and COBRA coverage, and 50% of the unvested portion of her equity awards will become vested. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to the terms of his offer letter agreement, upon a change in control of Eiger that requires a move of the company over 50 miles or results in a
substantial reduction in his responsibilities or compensation, Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer receives 12 months of base salary, six months of COBRA coverage and the unvested portion of his equity awards will immediately vest in full. Upon termination of his
employment without cause, Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer receives six months of base salary and COBRA coverage, and 50% of the unvested portion of his equity awards will become vested. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Employment, Severance and Change of Control Agreements with our Former Named Executive Officer </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Celladon entered into an amended and restated employment letter agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund in August 2013, as amended in January 2014, which became
effective in January 2014 in connection with the execution and </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">27 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
delivery of the underwriting agreement related to Celladon&#146;s initial public offering. Under the amended and restated letter agreement, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund was entitled to an initial annual base
salary of $200,000, was eligible to receive an annual target performance bonus as determined by the Board of Directors, and was entitled to certain severance benefits. In March 2014, the Compensation Committee and the Board of Directors reviewed the
salary and target bonus percentages for the executive officers and made certain changes. As approved by the Board of Directors, effective March&nbsp;1, 2014, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund was entitled to an annual base salary of $244,100 and was eligible to
receive an annual target performance bonus of up to 30% of his base salary as determined by the Board of Directors, and effective January&nbsp;1, 2015, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund was entitled to an annual base salary of $251,423. Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s
employment letter agreement was subsequently amended two times during 2015 as described below. In May 2015, Celladon entered into a Retention Agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund as described below and in November 2015, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s employment
letter agreement and Retention Agreement were terminated and replaced with an Executive Bonus Agreement, as described below. Also in November 2015, Celladon entered into a Merger Incentive Bonus Agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund, as described below.
Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s employment with Celladon terminated March&nbsp;22, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the terms of the Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s employment letter
agreement, upon his termination without &#147;cause,&#148; or resignation for &#147;good reason,&#148; each as defined in the Celladon Corporation 2013 Equity Incentive Plan, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund was eligible to receive continued base salary payments
and COBRA premium payments for nine months. If Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s termination without cause or resignation for good reason were to occur within the three-month period before or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-month</FONT> period following a
change of control, as defined under the Celladon Corporation 2013 Equity Incentive Plan, he would have been eligible to receive (1)&nbsp;continued base salary payments and COBRA premium payments for 12 months, (2)&nbsp;a lump sum payment equal to
his target bonus for the year of termination and (3)&nbsp;full vesting acceleration of all outstanding equity awards that are subject to time-based vesting. All severance benefits under Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s employee letter agreement were
contingent upon the named executive officer executing an effective release and waiver of claims against us. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>1st Amendment to Employment Agreement
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In May 2015, Celladon amended the letter agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund to provide that any cash severance would be paid as a lump sum, as opposed to
continued base salary payments as provided in the original terms of his employment letter agreement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>2nd Amendment to Employment Agreement </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On September&nbsp;25, 2015, Celladon&#146;s Board of Directors approved modifications to the severance arrangements of Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund, and on
October&nbsp;20, 2015, Celladon entered into an amendment to Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s employment letter agreement to memorialize the modified severance arrangements. In connection with Celladon&#146;s process of seeking a merger, sale or other
disposition of the company, Celladon&#146;s Board of Directors deemed it advisable, and in the best interests of Celladon&#146;s stockholders, to incentivize Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund to continue his employment with Celladon for an additional period of time.
Accordingly, the modified severance arrangements for Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund provided certainty that, if terminated by Celladon without &#147;cause&#148; or upon a resignation for &#147;good reason,&#148; Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund would receive the enhanced
severance benefits previously provided for in the event of such a qualifying termination occurring within three months prior to or twelve months following a change of control transaction (including a liquidation of Celladon). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Retention Program </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In April 2015, Celladon&#146;s Board
of Directors approved a reduction of Celladon&#146;s full-time workforce and committed to retention payments payable to certain key employees, if such employees remained with Celladon until December&nbsp;31, 2015 or were terminated by Celladon
without cause prior to such date (the &#147;Retention Program&#148;). The Retention Program was amended on May&nbsp;13, 2015 to add Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund, and on May&nbsp;27, 2015, Celladon entered into an agreement with Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund to memorialize
the terms of the amended Retention </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">28 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
Program. Under the Retention Agreement, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund was eligible to receive a lump sum retention payment equal to 50% of his base salary if he remained employed by Celladon until
December&nbsp;31, 2015, or if he was terminated by Celladon without cause prior to such date. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Bonus Payments in Lieu of Severance and Retention
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective November&nbsp;18, 2015, in conjunction with entering into the Merger Agreement with Eiger, Celladon entered into an agreement with
Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund providing for a cash bonus payment (an &#147;Executive Bonus Payment&#148;) to him in an amount equal to the cash severance and retention benefit payments provided in his previously existing employment letter agreement and Retention
Agreement (the &#147;Executive Bonus Agreements&#148;). The Executive Bonus Payment for Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund equaled the cash payment amount that he would have been entitled to under the terms of his employment agreement, as amended, and Retention
Agreement (collectively, the &#147;Prior Agreements&#148;) had he been terminated without cause or resigned for good reason (or, with respect to the Retention Agreements, remained employed by Celladon on December&nbsp;31, 2015), and replaced and
superseded each officer&#146;s right to any cash severance or retention benefits under the Prior Agreements. Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund&#146;s Executive Bonus Payment was subject to his delivery of an effective waiver and release of claims and was paid in
December 2015. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Merger Incentive Bonus Program </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Also
in connection with entering into the Merger Agreement with Eiger, Celladon adopted an incentive bonus program for Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund, pursuant to which he was eligible to receive incentive payments upon the achievement of the following key
merger-related milestones: (i)&nbsp;filing of the registration statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4</FONT> in respect of the proposed merger; (ii)&nbsp;mailing of the proxy statement/prospectus/information statement portion of such
registration statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-4</FONT> to the Celladon stockholders; and (iii)&nbsp;approval of the Merger by Celladon&#146;s stockholders. Subject to achievement and provided that he remained employed with
Celladon as of the date of such milestone achievement, Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund was eligible to receive a payment of $50,000 for each milestone. The milestone payments were paid upon achievement of each of the foregoing milestones to Mr.&nbsp;Wiklund. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Option Repricings </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We did not engage in any repricings or
other material modifications to any of our named executive officers&#146; outstanding equity awards during the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Perquisites, Health, Welfare and Retirement Benefits </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Eiger&#146;s named executive officers are eligible to participate in Eiger&#146;s employee benefit plans and programs, including medical and dental benefits,
flexible spending accounts, long-term care benefits, and short- and long-term disability and life insurance, to the same extent as its other full-time employees, subject to the terms and eligibility requirements of those plans. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Eiger maintains a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-qualified</FONT> retirement plan that provides eligible U.S. employees with an opportunity to save for
retirement on a tax advantaged basis. Eligible employees may defer eligible compensation subject to applicable annual Code limits. The 401(k) plan permits participants to make both <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> and certain <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> (Roth) deferral contributions. These contributions are allocated to each participant&#146;s individual account and are then invested in selected investment alternatives according to the participant&#146;s
directions. Employees are immediately and fully vested in their contributions. Currently, Eiger makes matching contributions to the 401(k) plan in the amount of up to 4% of each eligible U.S. employee&#146;s annual salary, subject to applicable
annual Code limits. The 401(k) plan is intended to be qualified under Section 401(a) of the Code with the 401(k) plan&#146;s related trust intended to be exempt under Section 501(a) of the Code. As a tax qualified retirement plan, contributions to
the 401(k) plan and earnings on those contributions are not taxable to the employees until distributed from the 401(k) plan. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">29 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Although Eiger does not have a formal policy with respect to the grant of equity incentive awards to its
executive officers or any formal equity ownership guidelines applicable to them, Eiger believes that equity grants provide its executives with a strong link to Eiger&#146;s long-term performance, create an ownership culture and help to align the
interests of Eiger&#146;s executives and its stockholders. In addition, Eiger believes that equity grants with a time-based vesting feature promote executive retention because this feature incentivizes executive officers to remain in Eiger&#146;s
employment during the vesting period. In 2016, Eiger granted Mr.&nbsp;Cory an option to purchase 285,991 shares of Eiger common stock, Dr.&nbsp;Quan an option to purchase 53,452 shares of its common stock and Mr.&nbsp;Shaffer an option to purchase
60,699 shares of Eiger common stock. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Nonqualified Deferred Compensation </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">None of Eiger&#146;s named executive officers participated in or had account balances in nonqualified defined contribution plans or other nonqualified deferred
compensation plans maintained by Eiger. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>E<SMALL>QUITY</SMALL> C<SMALL>OMPENSATION</SMALL> P<SMALL>LAN</SMALL> I<SMALL>NFORMATION</SMALL> </B></P>

will be three years from the date of termination of service, if such termination of service is other than for cause subject to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ten-year</FONT> term of each option. The options were granted under the
Company&#146;s 2013 Plan. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Private Eiger did not have a director compensation policy, and none of Private Eiger&#146;s directors, including those that
presently serve as directors of the Company, received compensation from Private Eiger during the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2016. However, Private Eiger provided reimbursement for reasonable out of pocket expenses incurred for attending meetings
of the Private Eiger board of directors. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">31 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>T<SMALL>RANSACTIONS</SMALL> W<SMALL>ITH</SMALL> R<SMALL>ELATED</SMALL> P<SMALL>ERSONS</SMALL>
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>R<SMALL>ELATED</SMALL>-<SMALL>PERSON</SMALL> T<SMALL>RANSACTIONS</SMALL> P<SMALL>OLICY</SMALL> <SMALL>AND</SMALL> P<SMALL>ROCEDURES</SMALL>
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We have adopted a written related-person transactions policy that sets forth our policies and procedures regarding the identification, review,
consideration and oversight of &#147;related-person transactions.&#148; For purposes of our policy only, a &#147;related-person transaction&#148; is a transaction, arrangement or relationship (or any series of similar transactions, arrangements or
relationships) in which we and any &#147;related person&#148; are participants involving an amount that exceeds $120,000. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transactions involving
compensation for services provided to us as an employee, consultant or director are not considered related-person transactions under this policy. A related person is any executive officer, director or a holder of more than 5% of our common stock,
including any of their immediate family members and any entity owned or controlled by such persons. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the policy, where a transaction has been
identified as a related-person transaction, management must present information regarding the proposed related-person transaction to our Audit Committee (or, where review by our Audit Committee would be inappropriate, to another independent body of
our Board of Directors) for review. The presentation must include a description of, among other things, the material facts, the direct and indirect interests of the related persons, the benefits of the transaction to us and whether any alternative
transactions are available. To identify related-person transactions in advance, we rely on information supplied by our executive officers, directors and certain significant stockholders. In considering related-person transactions, our Audit
Committee or another independent body of our Board of Directors takes into account the relevant available facts and circumstances including, but not limited to: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the risks, costs and benefits to us; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the impact on a director&#146;s independence in the event the related person is a director, immediate family member of a director or an entity with which a director is affiliated; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the terms of the transaction; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the availability of other sources for comparable services or products; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the terms available to or from, as the case may be, unrelated third parties or to or from our employees generally. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the event a director has an interest in the proposed transaction, the director must recuse himself or herself from the deliberations and approval. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>C<SMALL>ERTAIN</SMALL> R<SMALL>ELATIONSHIPS</SMALL> <SMALL>AND</SMALL> R<SMALL>ELATED</SMALL>-P<SMALL>ERSON</SMALL> T<SMALL>RANSACTIONS</SMALL> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following is a summary of transactions since January&nbsp;1, 2015 in which we have participated in which the amount involved exceeded or will exceed
$120,000, and in which any of our directors, executive officers or holders of more than 5% of our capital stock or any members of their immediate family had or will have a direct or indirect material interest, other than compensation arrangements
which are described under &#147;Executive Compensation&#148; and &#147;Director Compensation.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Eiger Bridge Financing </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In November 2015, Private Eiger entered into a convertible note and warrant purchase agreement (the &#147;Private Eiger Bridge Financing&#148;), in which
Private Eiger issued (i)&nbsp;convertible promissory notes (the &#147;Private Eiger Bridge Notes&#148;) for an aggregate principal amount of $6.0&nbsp;million, and (ii)&nbsp;warrants exercisable for shares of Private Eiger&#146;s equity securities
at a purchase price of $0.01 per share. The Private Eiger Bridge Notes accrued interest at a rate of 6% per year and had a maturity date of March&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Consists of (a) 405,411 shares to be purchased by Vivo Ventures Fund VI, L.P. and (b) 2,969 shares to be purchased by Vivo Ventures VI Affiliates Fund, L.P. Edgar Engleman is a member of the Company&#146;s board of
directors who has been designated by Vivo Ventures Fund VI, L.P. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Eiccose Asset Purchase Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In October 2015, Private Eiger entered into an Asset Purchase Agreement with Eiccose (the &#147;Eiccose APA&#148;). David Cory, the President, Chief Executive
Officer and a director of the Company, is the sole managing member and significant equity interest holder of Eiccose. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the Eiccose APA, Private
Eiger purchased all intellectual property rights with respect to ubenimex from Eiccose. Specifically, under the Eiccose APA, Eiccose assigned to Private Eiger the exclusive license agreement regarding ubenimex between Eiccose and Nippon Kayaku Co.,
Ltd., or the NK License. Private Eiger also purchased intellectual property rights related to Stanford Docket <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S11-438&#151;Pulmonary</FONT> Arterial Hypertension and Stanford Docket
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S14-323&#151;Lymphedema,</FONT> and Eiccose assigned to Private Eiger the exclusive license agreements between Eiccose and the Board of Trustees of Stanford regarding these two Stanford Dockets, or the Stanford
Licenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the terms of the Eiccose APA, at the closing of the financing on March&nbsp;22, 2016 pursuant to the Subscription Agreement referenced
above, Private Eiger issued to Eiccose 96,300 fully vested shares of Private Eiger common stock. Under the terms of the Eiccose APA, the Company is further required to pay Eiccose </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">33 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
milestone payments totaling up to $10.0&nbsp;million after achievement of specified milestones. The Company is also required to pay Eiccose royalties at a rate in the low single digits based on
the net sales of the first pharmaceutical product sold to an independent third party that contains or uses ubenimex. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the Eiccose APA, Private Eiger
also paid to Eiccose a total of $119,673, representing reimbursement of certain specified expenses, including payments and accrued amounts owed under the Stanford Licenses for previously incurred patent expenses and costs related to the negotiation
and assignment of the Stanford Licenses. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">34 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>H<SMALL>OUSEHOLDING</SMALL> <SMALL>OF</SMALL> P<SMALL>ROXY</SMALL> M<SMALL>ATERIALS</SMALL>
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The SEC has adopted rules that permit companies and intermediaries (e.g., brokers) to satisfy the delivery requirements for Annual Meeting materials
with respect to two or more stockholders sharing the same address by delivering a single set of Annual Meeting materials addressed to those stockholders. This process, which is commonly referred to as &#147;householding,&#148; potentially means
extra convenience for stockholders and cost savings for companies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This year, a number of brokers with account holders who are Eiger stockholders will be
&#147;householding&#148; the Company&#146;s proxy materials. A single set of Annual Meeting materials will be delivered to multiple stockholders sharing an address unless contrary instructions have been received from the affected stockholders. Once
you have received notice from your broker that they will be &#147;householding&#148; communications to your address, &#147;householding&#148; will continue until you are notified otherwise or until you revoke your consent. If, at any time, you no
longer wish to participate in &#147;householding&#148; and would prefer to receive a separate set of Annual Meeting materials, please notify your broker or Eiger. Direct your written request to Eiger BioPharmaceuticals, Inc., James Welch, Chief
Financial Officer, 350 Cambridge Ave., Suite 350, Palo Alto, CA 94306 or contact Mr.&nbsp;Welch at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">650-272-6138.</FONT></FONT> Stockholders who currently receive multiple copies of
the Annual Meeting materials at their addresses and would like to request &#147;householding&#148; of their communications should contact their brokers. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">35 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>O<SMALL>THER</SMALL> M<SMALL>ATTERS</SMALL> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board of Directors knows of no other matters that will be presented for consideration at the Annual Meeting.&nbsp;If any other matters are properly
brought before the meeting, it is the intention of the persons named in the accompanying proxy to vote on such matters in accordance with their best judgment. </P>
